Synthesis Subset of EVODEX-E

This table lists a subset of EVODEX-E operators optimized for pathway synthesis applications. The subset was created by removing ubiquitous metabolites from all reactions to derive partial reactions, which were then matched with comprehensive EVODEX-P members. This listing focuses on primary reaction changes without including cofactors or other universal metabolites.
